# <a name="release-notes-for-semi-annual-channel-releases-in-2017"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-103">2017中的半年频道发布的发行说明</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-103">Release notes for Semi-Annual Channel releases in 2017</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d47b1-104">这些发行说明提供了有关在2017中的 Office 365 专业增强版的半年频道更新中包含的新功能、安全更新和非安全更新的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-104">These release notes provide information about new features, security updates, and non-security updates that are included in Semi-Annual Channel updates to Office 365 ProPlus in 2017.</span></span> 
> [!NOTE]
> - <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-105">以下说明还提供了有关 Visio Pro for Office 365 和 Project Online 桌面客户端的新功能、安全更新和非安全更新的信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-105">The following also provides information about new features, security updates, and non-security updates for Visio Pro for Office 365 and Project Online Desktop Client.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-106">此信息还适用于 Office 365 商业版，即随附一些 Office 365 计划的 Office 版本（如企业高级版）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-106">This information also applies to Office 365 Business, which is the version of Office that comes with some Office 365 plans, such as Business Premium.</span></span>
> - <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-107">在 2018 年 1 月前，半年频道被命名为延期频道。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-107">Semi-Annual Channel was named Deferred Channel prior to January 2018.</span></span>

### <a name="access-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-172">Access：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-172">Access: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p101">**新增功能对话框：** 在 Access 更新了新功能后，打开 Access 时，会显示一个突出显示新 Access 功能的对话框。此外，还可以通过转到“文件”\>“帐户”\>“新增功能”找到此对话框。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p101">**What’s New dialog:** A dialog box that highlights new Access features appears when Access is opened after Access is updated with new features. The dialog box is also available by going to File \> Account \> What’s New.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p102">**支持大数 (bigint)：** 使用 Access 表中的 Large Number 数据类型来计算大型数字，并链接到使用等效数据类型的外部数据库（如 SQL Server 中的 bigint）或从中导入。 [详细信息](https://blogs.office.com/2017/03/06/new-in-access-2016-large-number-bigint-support/)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p102">**Large Number (bigint) support:** Use the Large Number data type in Access tables to calculate large numbers, and to link to or import from external databases that use an equivalent data type, such as bigint in SQL Server. [More information](https://blogs.office.com/2017/03/06/new-in-access-2016-large-number-bigint-support/)</span></span>

### <a name="excel-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-177">Excel：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-177">Excel: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-178">**Windows 信息保护 (WIP) 支持：**   Excel 现在是一个智能型应用，可以区分企业数据和个人数据，并根据配置的策略正确地确定要保护的数据。  [详细信息](https://aka.ms/wiptechnet)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-178">**Windows Information Protection (WIP) support:**   Excel is now an enlightened app, and can differentiate between corporate and personal data, correctly determining which to protect, based on configured policies.  [More information](https://aka.ms/wiptechnet)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p103">**“获取和转换数据”改进：** 在“查询编辑器”中，可以通过提供示例值创建新列。在输入过程中，Excel 会检测所需的转换，然后显示新列的预览效果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p103">**Get & Transform improvement:** In the Query Editor, create a new column by providing sample values. As you type, Excel detects the required transformations and shows a preview of the new column.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p104">**插入最近使用的链接：** 轻松地将超链接附加到最近使用的基于云的文件或网站，并为使用屏幕阅读器的用户创建有意义的显示名称。 [详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/002684c4-bf06-422b-821f-b4ef84fdb0e3)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p104">**Insert recent links:** Easily attach hyperlinks to recent cloud-based files or websites, and create meaningful display names for people using screen readers. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/002684c4-bf06-422b-821f-b4ef84fdb0e3)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p105">**个性化设置默认的数据透视表布局：** 以你喜欢的方式设置数据透视表，并在每次创建新的数据透视表时从该布局开始。 [更多信息](https://support.office.com/article/efd8569c-f07a-43c1-9db2-4f2912a0f94e)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p105">**Personalize the default PivotTable layout:** Set up a PivotTable the way you like, and start with that layout every time you create a new PivotTable. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/efd8569c-f07a-43c1-9db2-4f2912a0f94e)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p106">**“获取和转换”改进：** 用户可以通过示例创建新列，并将表列拆分为行。现在可以更轻松地为 SAP HANA 指定参数，以及进行数据分组了。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p106">**Get & Transform improvements:** Users can create new columns by example and split table columns into rows. Specifying parameters to SAP HANA and grouping data is now easier.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p107">**外接程序的集中式部署**：管理员可以从 Office 365 管理中心将加载项部署并更新到用户或组。 [更多信息](https://dev.office.com/docs/add-ins/publish/centralized-deployment)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p107">**Centralized deployment of add-ins**: Admins can deploy and update add-ins to users or groups from the Office 365 admin center. [More information](https://dev.office.com/docs/add-ins/publish/centralized-deployment)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-189">**快速访问工具栏自定义：** 可将“下标”和“上标”图标添加至快速访问工具栏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-189">**Quick Access Toolbar customization:** The Subscript and Superscript icons can be added to the Quick Access Toolbar.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-190">**“获取和转换”改进：** 使用查询编辑器拆分列时自动检测分隔符字符，选择要与合并二进制数据一起使用的示例文件，并指定使用 DB2 连接器时要连接的包集合。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-190">**Get & Transform improvements:** Automatic detection of delimiter character when splitting columns using the Query Editor, choose which sample file to use with Combine Binaries, and specify the package collection to connect to when using the DB2 Connector.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p108">**迪拜字体：** 支持西欧语言和使用阿拉伯语脚本的主要语言的字体系列。 [更多信息](https://support.office.com/article/c862df16-ae0d-46d9-b117-aa3f41f9706e)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p108">**Dubai font:** Font family that supports both Western European languages as well as the major languages that use the Arabic script. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/c862df16-ae0d-46d9-b117-aa3f41f9706e)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-193">**背景消除：** 使用任意格式的绘图工具删除图片背景。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-193">**Background removal:** Remove a picture background with a free-form drawing tool.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-194">**“获取和转换”改进：** 在“导航器”对话框中通过 ODCB 和 OLEDB 连接器使用“选择相关表”，直接从文件夹“数据预览”对话框中合并多个文件，并在“查询编辑器”窗口中使用新的上下文菜单选项在现有查询中插入新步骤。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-194">**Get & Transform improvements:** Use “Select Related Tables” in the Navigator dialog with the ODCB and OLEDB connectors, combine multiple files directly from the folder Data Preview dialog, and use a new context menu option in the Query Editor window to insert new steps in existing queries.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-195">**使用触笔选择和更改对象：** 使用数字触笔捕捉对象句柄，以执行重设大小、旋转、移动等操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-195">**Use a pen to select and change objects:** Grab object handles with a digital pen to resize, rotate, move, and more.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p109">**地图图表：** 跨地理区域比较值和显示类别。 [更多信息](https://support.office.com/article/f2cfed55-d622-42cd-8ec9-ec8a358b593b)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p109">**Map Chart:** Compare values and show categories across geographic regions. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/f2cfed55-d622-42cd-8ec9-ec8a358b593b)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p110">**SVG 图像：** 在工作簿中插入和编辑可缩放的矢量图形 (SVG)。 [详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/69f29d39-194a-4072-8c35-dbe5e7ea528c)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p110">**SVG images:** Insert and edit scalable vector graphics (SVG) in workbooks. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/69f29d39-194a-4072-8c35-dbe5e7ea528c)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-200">**插入图标：**  通过转到插入插图图标 (SVG) 文件的标准库中的图标（通过可缩放的矢量图形） \> \> 。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-200">**Insert icons:**  Use icons from a standard library of scalable vector graphics (SVG) files by going to Insert \> Illustrations \> Icons.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="d47b1-201">详细信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-201">More information</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/e2459f17-3996-4795-996e-b9a13486fa79)
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-202">**保存到最近访问的文件夹：** 依次转到“文件”\>“另存为”，使用“最近访问的位置”选项卡，将工作簿保存到最近访问的文件夹中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-202">**Save to Recent folders:** Save a workbook to a recently used folder by using the Recent tab when you go to File \> Save As.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p112">**辅助功能改进：** 改进了支持，可以更好地使用键盘、讲述人和其他辅助技术阅读和编辑工作簿。 [更多信息](https://support.office.com/article/51fcb17a-b15b-4b13-ae04-d4f38ece3f78)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p112">**Accessibility improvements:** Improved support for using the keyboard, Narrator, and other assistive technology to read and edit workbooks. ### <a name="excel-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-211">Excel：非安全更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-211">Excel: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-212">修复了复制和粘贴到 Excel（如忽略制表符分隔的 HTML 文本）、错误地删除空行和列、忽略对齐方式和忽略公式这些问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-212">Fix issues with copying and pasting into Excel, such as ignoring tab-separated HTML text, incorrectly removing empty rows and columns, ignoring alignment, and ignoring formulas.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-213">修复了以下问题：在尝试将更改保存到与 OneDrive 客户端同步的文档时出现错误。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-213">Fix an issue where errors appear when trying to save changes to documents synchronized with the OneDrive client.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-214">修复了以下问题：将工作表数据添加到数据模型，并将“高对比度”主题设置为“黑色”时，Excel 发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-214">Fix an issue where Excel crashes when adding worksheet data to a Data Model and the High Contrast theme is set to Black.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-215">修复了由于工作簿包含外部链接而导致 Excel 崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-215">Fix an issue where Excel crashes for workbooks that contain external links.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-216">修复了即使未选择“在具有零值的单元格中显示零”设置，将单元格从 Excel 粘贴到 Word 也在单元格中显示零的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-216">Fix an issue where pasting cells from Excel to Word shows zeros in the cells, even though the "Show a zero in cells that have zero value" setting is not selected.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-217">修复了以下问题：以编程方式为使用 Excel 2010 或更低版本创建的工作簿应用工作表保护密码时，Excel 无法设置此密码。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-217">Fix an issue where Excel doesn't set the sheet protection password when applied programmatically for workbooks created in Excel 2010 or earlier.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-218">修复了以下问题：“合并后居中”对分组的工作表无效。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-218">Fix an issue where Merge & Center doesn't work in grouped worksheets.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-219">修复了以下问题：缺少在 Office 2016 发布后引入的新函数，例如 TEXTJOIN、CONCAT、IFS、MAXIFS 和 MINIFS。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-219">Fix an issue where new functions that were introduced after the release of Office 2016 - for example, TEXTJOIN, CONCAT, IFS, MAXIFS, and MINIFS - are missing.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-220">修复了以下问题：Excel 在用户尝试应用单元格级权限时出现故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-220">Fix an issue where Excel crashes when the user attempts to apply cell level permissions.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-221">修复了以下问题：将大型文件保存到 OneDrive for Business 导致文件锁定并且用户无法编辑该文件直到用户关闭并重新打开 Excel。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-221">Fix an issue where saving a large file to OneDrive for Business causes the file to be locked and the user can't edit the file until the user closes and reopens Excel.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-222">修复了以下问题：打开 .xls 工作簿时，新窗口显示为灰色。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-222">Fix an issue where a new window appears grayed out when an .xls workbook is opened.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-223">修复了以下问题：Excel 可能会在用户插入超链接时发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-223">Fix an issue where Excel might crash when inserting hyperlinks.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-224">修复了在添加 XML 映射时 Excel 可能发生故障的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-224">Fix an issue where Excel might fail when adding XML Maps.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-225">修复了外接程序升级后或从 Office 应用商店中删除并再次下载该外接程序后，外接程序的命令按钮不起作用的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-225">Fix an issue where the command button for an Add-in doesn't work after the add-in is upgraded or after removing and downloading the Add-in again from the Office store.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-226">修复了以下问题：通过 VBA 控制 DLL 工作表时，Excel 可能会发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-226">Fix an issue where Excel might crash when manipulating DLL sheets via VBA.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-227">修复了以下问题：选择图表工作表上的表单控件组合框时，Excel 可能会发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-227">Fix an issue where Excel crashes when selecting a form control combo box on a chart sheet.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-302">修复了以下问题：如果有特定的西班牙语区域设置，无法将任务开始日期和完成日期正确同步到 SharePoint 任务列表中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-302">Fix an issue where task start and finish dates don't synchronize to a SharePoint tasks list correctly if you have certain Spanish regional settings.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-303">修复了以下问题：如果从 Project 客户端启动状态审批流程，可能永远无法完成，导致项目处于不可用状态。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-303">Fix an issue where if you initiate the status approvals process from the Project client, it may never finish, leaving the project in an unusable state.</span></span>

### <a name="skype-for-business-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-332">Skype for Business：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-332">Skype for Business: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-333">**插入链接：** 可以在 IM 和群组聊天中添加链接，并输入易记的链接文本，而不是完整 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-333">**Insert link:** Add a link into IM and group chats and provide friendly text for the link instead of the full URL.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p126">**屏幕共享通知：** 在 IM 对话中共享屏幕或在离开会议后仍继续共享屏幕时，对话窗口中会显示屏幕共享通知。此通知旨在提醒仍在共享屏幕，只需使用“停止共享”按钮，即可轻松停止共享。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p126">**Screen sharing notification:** A notification displays in the conversation window when you’re sharing a screen in an IM conversation or when screen sharing continues after you leave a meeting. The notification reminds you that you are still sharing your screen and makes it easy to stop sharing by using the “Stop Sharing” button.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-336">**Windows 信息保护 (WIP) 支持：** Skype for Business 现作为“仅 WIP 作业”应用受到支持。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-336">**Windows Information Protection (WIP) support:** Skype for Business is now supported as a WIP-work only app.</span></span><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-337">通过将 Skype 添加到允许的应用列表，可以指示 Windows 不处理个人数据。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-337">  By adding Skype to your allowed apps list, it indicates to Windows that it does not handle personal data.</span></span><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-338">Windows 将代表 Skype for Business 保护数据。  [详细信息](https://aka.ms/wiptechnet)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-338">  Windows will protect data on behalf of Skype for Business.  [More information](https://aka.ms/wiptechnet)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-339">**密码重置选项：** 当用户至少登录失败一次时，重置按钮链接将显示在登录窗口中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-339">**Password reset option:** A reset button link appears on the sign in window when a user fails to sign in at least once.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-371">修复了用户右键单击与会者列表中的其他用户名字时会议名单的第一行为空白的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-371">Fix an issue where the first line of the meeting roster is blank when a user right-clicks on another user's name in the participant list.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-372">修复了以下问题：用户在切换内外公司网络后无法登录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-372">Fix an issue where users are unable to sign in when switching between inside and outside corporate networks.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-373">修复了在咨询转接中从 IM 升级到音频时，聊天区域不会关闭的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-373">Fix an issue where the chat region does not close when escalating from IM to Audio in Consultative Transfer.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-374">修复了所使用的两个端点同时响铃时，toast 通知中的名称被截断的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-374">Fix an issue where names are truncated in toast notifications when simultaneous ringing of two endpoints is used.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-375">修复了共享通知时，文件中的文件名被截断的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-375">Fix an issue where the file name is truncated in file sharing notifications.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-376">添加“返回通话”和转接按钮的工具提示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-376">Add tool tips for Back to Call and transfer buttons.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-377">使“咨询转接”窗口的保持时间用于屏幕阅读器（如讲述人）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-377">Make the time spent on hold in the consultative transfer window available to screen readers, such as Narrator.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-378">添加了可选择 IM 或呼叫作为咨询转接的默认首选项的功能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-378">Add the ability to choose either IM or calls as the default preference for consultative transfer.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-379">添加了以下功能：进行咨询式呼叫转移时，右键单击“转接”按钮可以查看联系人的电话号码列表。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-379">Add the ability, when doing a consultative transfer, to right-click the "Transfer" button to see a list of phone numbers for the contact.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-380">改进了常见错误消息，以表明问题在于用户具有无效的许可证还是尚未分配许可证。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-380">Improve a general error message to make it clear that the problem is that the user has an invalid license or hasn't been assigned a license.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-381">修复了当用户开始与联系人进行对话，然后添加其他联系人时，并非所有联系人都显示在对话窗口标题中的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-381">Fix an issue where not all the contacts are displayed in the conversation window title when a user starts a conversation with a contact and then adds another contact.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-382">修复了讲述人不读取通知第 2 行的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-382">Fix an issue where Narrator doesn't read the 2nd line of notifications.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-383">修复了呼叫转移到 VOIP 而不是咨询的号码的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-383">Fix an issue where calls are transferred to VOIP instead of the consulted number.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-384">修复了当用户在“内容”窗口中导航时，讲述者宣布不正确的信息的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-384">Fix an issue where Narrator announces incorrect information when the user is navigating in the Content window.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-385">修复了以下问题：将鼠标悬停在白板注释上时，看不到创建者和修改者名称</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-385">Fix an issue where the creator and modifier names don't appear when hovering over an annotation on a whiteboard</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p130">**插入最近使用的链接：** 将超链接附加到最近使用的基于云的文件或网站，并为使用屏幕阅读器的用户创建有意义的显示名称。 [更多信息](https://support.office.com/article/002684c4-bf06-422b-821f-b4ef84fdb0e3)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p130">**Insert recent links:** Attach hyperlinks to recent cloud-based files or websites, and create meaningful display names for people using screen readers. ### <a name="excel-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-488">Excel：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-488">Excel: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-489">**改进了数据转换和连接性：** 将列表扩展为在各值之间使用分隔符的新文本列，并在连接 SQL 时指定故障转移选项。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-489">**Data transformation and connectivity enhancements:** Expand a list into a new text column with delimiter between the values, and specify a failover option when connecting to SQL.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-490">**改进了数据转换和连接性：** 现在支持百分比数据类型，并改进了二进制组合和函数创作体验。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-490">**Data transformation and connectivity enhancements:** The Percentage data type is now supported, and binary combining function authoring experiences have been enhanced.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-491">**OLEDB 连接器：** 在“获取并转换”中使用 OLEDB 连接器创建查询以导入数据，具体方法为指定连接字符串和要执行 SQL 语句（可选）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-491">**OLEDB connector:** Use the OLEDB connector in Get & Transform to create a query to import data by specifying a Connection String and, optionally, a SQL statement to execute.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p136">**墨迹重播：** 依次转到“绘图”\>“墨迹重播”，可以向前和向后重播手写内容以隐藏和显示内容，也可以提供分步说明或更好地理解其他人的思路。 [更多信息](https://support.office.com/article/fa4f044f-810b-43fe-b774-da04a0b37496)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p136">**Ink replay:** Go to Draw \> Ink Replay to replay handwriting forward and backward to hide and reveal content, provide step-by-step instructions, or better understand the flow of others’ thoughts. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/fa4f044f-810b-43fe-b774-da04a0b37496)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-494">**CSV (UTF-8) 支持：** 打开和保存使用 UTF-8 字符编码的 CSV 文件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-494">**CSV (UTF-8) support:** Open and save CSV files that use UTF-8 character encoding.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-495">**增强了数据转换功能和连接性：** 从 OData 源加载数据时选择导入相关表，添加包含函数计算值的自定义列，或使用专用视图展示查询之间的依赖关系。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-495">**Data Transformations and Connectivity Enhancements:** Select to import related tables when loading data from OData sources, add custom columns with values coming from a function computation, or show the dependencies between queries using a dedicated view.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p137">**与我共享的内容：** 依次转到“文件”\>“打开”\>“与我共享的内容”，查看其他人与你共享的文档。 [详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/e0476dc7-bf2f-4203-b9ad-c809578b03e7)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p137">**Shared with Me:** See documents others have shared with you by going to File \> Open \> Shared with Me. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/e0476dc7-bf2f-4203-b9ad-c809578b03e7)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p138">**更改颜色：** 使用“操作说明搜索”来设置字体、突出显示、形状填充等的颜色。 [更多信息](https://support.office.com/article/5bab7082-b772-427c-a106-14ae46f8687f)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p138">**Change colors:** Use Tell Me to set the color for the font, highlighting, shape fill, and more. ### <a name="excel-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-503">Excel：非安全更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-503">Excel: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-504">修复了以下问题：当加载表的列名称中有尾随空格时，模块查询刷新失败。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-504">Fix an issue where a model query refresh fails when the loaded table has a trailing whitespace in the column name.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-505">修复了以下问题：打开 .xls 工作簿时，新窗口灰显。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-505">Fix an issue where a new window appears grayed out when an .xls workbook is opened.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-506">修复了以下问题：Excel 可能会在用户插入超链接时发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-506">Fix an issue where Excel might crash when inserting hyperlinks.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-507">修复了在添加 XML 映射时 Excel 可能发生故障的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-507">Fix an issue where Excel might fail when adding XML Maps.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-508">修复了外接程序升级后或从 Office 应用商店中删除并再次下载该外接程序后，外接程序的命令按钮不起作用的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-508">Fix an issue where the command button for an Add-in doesn't work after the add-in is upgraded or after removing and downloading the Add-in again from the Office store.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-509">修复了通过 VBA 操作 DLL 工作表时 Excel 可能崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-509">Fix an issue where Excel might crash when manipulating DLL sheets via VBA.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-510">修复了以下问题：如果 Office 主题设为“黑色”，用户在“工作簿查询”窗格中右键单击查询时会看到内容为“意外错误”的错误消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-510">Fix an issue where, when the Office theme is set to Black, an "Unexpected Error" error message appears when right-clicking on a query in the Workbook Queries pane.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-511">修复了以下问题：Excel 在用户尝试访问数据透视表选项时发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-511">Fix an issue where Excel crashes when the user tries to access PivotTable Options.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-512">修复了以下问题：在另存为 CSV 或 CSV UTF-8 时，无法正确导出包含文本和双引号的单元格值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-512">Fix an issue where cell values with text and double quotes aren't correctly exported when saving as CSV or CSV UTF-8.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-513">修复了以下问题：Excel 在关闭时挂起或发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-513">Fix an issue where Excel hangs or crashes when closing.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-514">修复了以下问题：包含连接公式的超链接忽略部分连接结果。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-514">Fix an issue where a hyperlink containing a concatenate formula ignores part of the concatenate result.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-515">修复了以下问题：在 Word 中粘贴 RTF 格式 Excel 表格时，无法保留表格格式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-515">Fix an issue where pasting an Excel table in rich text format (RTF) to Word doesn't preserve the table format.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-516">修复了以下问题：当工作簿包含 MS Excel 4.0 宏工作表时，用户无法另存为。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-516">Fix an issue where the user can't perform a Save As when the workbook contains a MS Excel 4.0 Macro worksheet.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-517">设置 CTRL+ALT+5 快捷键，用于将选定内容移到对象层，以与其他应用程序保持一致。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-517">Make CTRL+ALT+5 the shortcut for moving a selection to the object layer to match other applications.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-518">修复了以下问题：在编辑栏中键入内容并使用带下拉列表的函数（如 VLOOKUP）时，如果按下 Enter 完成公式，系统会选择自动完成下拉列表中最上面一项，而不是原封不动地保留所键入的值。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-518">Fix an issue where, when typing in the formula bar and using a function with a dropdown, such as VLOOKUP, hitting Enter to complete the formula selects the top item from the autocomplete dropdown instead of leaving the typed in value as-is.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-519">修复了以下问题：打开受保护的工作表中有超链接的 Excel 97-Excel 2003 二进制文件格式 (BIFF8) 文件时，Excel 认为文件已损坏，并尝试修复或删除不可读取的内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-519">Fix an issue where opening an Excel 97 - Excel 2003 Binary file format (BIFF8) file that contains a hyperlink in a protected sheet causes Excel to think the file is corrupt and Excel tries to repair or remove the unreadable content.</span></span>

### <a name="onedrive-for-business-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-520">OneDrive for Business：非安全更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-520">OneDrive for Business: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-521">修复了以下问题：在无法成功加载 GrooveIntlResource.dll 的情况下（通常不太可能会发生这种情况），如果用户尝试打开文件或将文件保存到同步文件夹，Office 应用可能会发生故障，或者如果用户使用 Windows 资源管理器转到同步文件夹，Windows 资源管理器可能会发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-521">Fix an issue where, if the GrooveIntlResource.dll can't be loaded successfully (which is unlikely under normal circumstances), an Office app can crash if the user tries to open or save a file to a synced folder, or Windows Explorer can crash if the user navigates to a synced folder by using Windows Explorer.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-522">修复了以下问题：如果将 Office 配置为从除 Office 内容传送网络 (CDN) 之外的位置接收更新程序，无法禁用 OneDrive for Business，即使将相应的注册表项设置为禁用它，也是如此。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-522">Fix an issue where OneDrive for Business is not disabled, even though the appropriate registry key is set to disable it, when Office is configured to receive updates from a location other than the Office Content Delivery Network (CDN).</span></span>

### <a name="outlook-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-543">Outlook：非安全更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-543">Outlook: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-544">修复了删除消息时导致用户间歇性地看到消息列表中的所选消息意外跳转的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-544">Fix an issue that causes users to intermittently see the message selection in the message list jump unexpectedly when deleting messages.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-550">修复了以下问题：收件人无法打开使用信息权限管理予以发送的 RTF 格式电子邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-550">Fix an issue where Rich Text Format (RTF) e-mail messages can't be opened by the recipient if the message was sent using Information Rights Management.</span></span>

### <a name="powerpoint-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-551">PowerPoint：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-551">PowerPoint: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-552">**隐藏式字幕：** 如果幻灯片中的视频包含隐藏式字幕，可在幻灯片中播放这些字幕。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-552">**Closed captions:** If a slide contains a video that has closed captions, the captions can be played in the slideshow.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p142">**与我共享的内容：** 依次转到“文件”\>“打开”\>“与我共享的内容”，查看其他人与你共享的文档。 [更多信息](https://support.office.com/article/e0476dc7-bf2f-4203-b9ad-c809578b03e7)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p142">**Shared with Me:** See documents others have shared with you by going to File \> Open \> Shared with Me. -   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p143">**墨迹重播：** 可以向前和向后重播手写内容以隐藏和显示内容，也可以提供分步说明或更好地理解其他人的思路。 [详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/fa4f044f-810b-43fe-b774-da04a0b37496)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p143">**Ink replay:** Replay handwriting forward and backward to hide and reveal content, provide step-by-step instructions, or better understand the flow of others’ thoughts. You can also embed quizzes to assist with remote learning and make your presentation more interactive as well as change the ink color and use simpler controls to record narrations and audio.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-561">**设计器改进：** 提供了针对加点符的流程列表使用 SmartArt 的设计建议。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-561">**Designer improvements:** Provides design suggestions using SmartArt for bulleted process lists.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p145">**更改颜色：** 使用“操作说明搜索”来设置字体、突出显示、形状填充等的颜色。 [详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/5bab7082-b772-427c-a106-14ae46f8687f)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p145">**Change colors:** Use Tell Me to set the color for the font, highlighting, shape fill, and more. -   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p146">**缩放：** 创建带有自动导航链接的演示文稿交互式摘要。 [更多信息](https://support.office.com/article/9d6c58cd-2125-4d29-86b1-0097c7dc47d7)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p146">**Zoom:** Create an interactive summary of your presentation with automatic navigation links. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/9d6c58cd-2125-4d29-86b1-0097c7dc47d7)</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-567">**打开超链接：** 使用 CTRL+单击，在编辑演示文稿时打开超链接。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-567">**Opening hyperlinks:** Use CTRL+click to open hyperlinks when editing a presentation.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-568">**文本突出显示：** 使用文本荧光笔突出显示重要文本。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-568">**Text highlighting:** Draw attention to important text by using the text highlighter.</span></span>

### <a name="powerpoint-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-569">PowerPoint：非安全更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-569">PowerPoint: Non-security updates</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-580">修复了以下问题：当包含嵌入字体的文件自动保存时，文本键入发生中断和延迟。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-580">Fix an issue where typing text is interrupted and delayed when a file that has embedded fonts is auto saved.</span></span>

### <a name="project-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-582">Project：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-582">Project: Feature updates</span></span>

### <a name="skype-for-business-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-623">Skype for Business：非安全更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-623">Skype for Business: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-624">修复了导致自动接受的对话的对话窗口以普通窗口而不是最小化窗口模式打开，并意外地将焦点从其他窗口移开的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-624">Fix an issue that causes a conversation window for an automatically accepted conversation to open as a normal window, instead of minimized, and unexpectedly take focus away from other windows.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-625">修复了以下问题：用户在切换内外公司网络后无法登录。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-625">Fix an issue where users are unable to sign in when switching between inside and outside corporate networks.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-626">将用来允许或拒绝参与者的介绍按钮从文本更改为图像（X 或选中标记）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-626">Change the lobby buttons used to admit or deny participants from text to images (an X or a checkmark).</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-627">将会议提醒通知文本从“接受”更改为“加入”。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-627">Change the meeting reminder notification text from "Accept" to "Join."</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-628">更新了 IM 发件人在收件人的状态设置为“请勿打扰”时看到的消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-628">Update the message shown to the sender of an IM when the recipient's status is set to Do Not Disturb.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-629">更新了 IM 发件人在收件人处于脱机状态且已禁用“保存到历史记录”时看到的消息，以明确指出收件人不会收到消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-629">Update the message shown to the sender of an IM, when the recipient is offline and "saving to history" is disabled, to make it clear that the recipient won't receive the message.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-630">新增以下功能：移动组聊天的聊天历史记录和名单之间的垂直拆分栏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-630">Add the capability to move the vertical splitter bar between the chat history and the roster in a group chat.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-631">新增以下功能：在 IM 或聊天室窗口中调整选项卡列表的大小。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-631">Add the capability to resize the list of tabs in IM or chat room windows.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-632">新增以下功能：在创建主题源时选择搜索到的聊天室。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-632">Add the capability to select the chat rooms searched when creating a topic feed.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-633">修复了以下问题：在对话中途，在聊天历史记录中看不到消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-633">Fix an issue where message stop appearing in chat history mid-conversation.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-634">修复了以下问题：对话窗口显示重复消息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-634">Fix an issue where duplicate messages appear in the conversation window.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-635">修复了以下问题：在有大量通知的情况下，toast 通知操作（“接受”和“忽略”）不会正确显示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-635">Fix an issue where toast notification actions (Accept and Ignore) aren't properly displayed during a high volume of notifications.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p152">修复了以下问题：当 Skype for Business 通过端口 443 连接到 SIP 服务器且存在代理服务器时，如果代理不允许此类连接，登录过程会明显延迟。通过在 HKEY\_CURRENT\_USER\\Software\\Microsoft\\UCCPlatform\\Lync 下添加 EnableDetectProxyForAllConnections DWORD 注册表项，并将值设置为 1，可以启用修复程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p152">Fix an issue where, when Skype for Business connects to a SIP server over port 443 and a proxy server is present, there is a significant delay in the sign-in process if the proxy doesn't allow such connections. ### <a name="office-suite-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-754">Office 套件：非安全更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-754">Office suite: Non-security updates</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-758">修复了以下问题：在 Office 文档中插入 SVG 图像后，SVG 图像在文档保存和重新打开后消失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-758">Fix an issue where, after inserting an SVG image in an Office document, the SVG image disappears when the document is saved and re-opened.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-761">修复了以下问题：配置管理器触发的更新将注册表中的 UpdateChannel 设置更改为不是有效更新通道的内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-761">Fix an issue where an update trigged by Configuration Manager changes the UpdateChannel setting in the registry to something that's not a valid update channel.</span></span>

### <a name="excel-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-847">Excel：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-847">Excel: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-848">**数据转换和连接性方面的增强功能：** 向查询添加参数，在合并或追加操作中创建新查询，以及使用 Web 连接器预览 Web 页。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-848">**Data Transformation and Connectivity enhancements:** Add parameters to queries, create new queries from Merge or Append operations, and use the Web connector to preview web pages.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-849">**图表的宏录制：** 支持树状图、直方图、排列图、瀑布图和箱形图。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-849">**Macro recording for charts:** Support for Treemap, Histogram, Pareto, Waterfall, and Box & Whisker charts.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-850">**保留了 Power Query 布局：** 查询刷新后，保留了使用获取和转换导入的数据的格式和计算列。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-850">**Power Query layouts preserved:** Formats and calculated columns for data imported using Get & Transform are preserved after queries refresh.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-851">**数据转换和连接性方面的改进：** 执行其他日期/时间转换和文本操作、将工作簿迁移到不同的环境、将两个或多个子句组合以进行行筛选以及在“查询编辑器”窗口中记录转换。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-851">**Data transformation and connectivity improvements:** Perform additional Date/Time transformation and Text manipulations, migrate workbooks to a different environment, group two or more clauses for row filtering, and document transformations within the Query Editor window.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-852">**发布到 Power BI：** 通过 Power BI 订阅将本地存储的文件发布到 Power BI。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-852">**Publish to Power BI:** Publish locally stored files to Power BI, with a Power BI subscription.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-853">**形状识别：** 将你的绘图自动转换为形状。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-853">**Shape Recognition:** Automatically transform your drawings into shapes.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-854">**新连接器：** 使用新联机服务类别（包括连接到 SharePoint Online、Exchange 和 SAP HANA 的连接器）中的选项创建查询。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-854">**New connectors:** Create a query using options from the new Online Services category including connectors to SharePoint Online, Exchange, and SAP HANA.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-855">**具有 OLAP 连接的数据透视表：** 改进了你创建、编辑、刷新具有 OLAP 连接的数据透视表时的性能。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-855">**PivotTables with OLAP connections:** Improved the performance when you create, edit, and refresh PivotTables with OLAP connections.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-856">**数据转换改进：** 可将持续时间值转换为年；支持在查询编辑器预览中使用空格和换行；以及可直接从查询窗格重命名查询。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-856">**Data transformation improvements:** Convert duration values to years, support for whitespace and line feeds in Query Editor preview, and rename queries directly from the Queries pane.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-857">**数据连接改进：** 可检测交错的 CSV 文件；支持在使用 Exchange 连接器时通过 Microsoft 帐户进行身份验证；以及可在尝试连接到用户的 SharePoint 列表时验证其提供的 URL。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-857">**Data connectivity improvements:** Detect jagged CSV files, support for authentication with a Microsoft account when using the Exchange connector, and validate URLs provided by users when trying to connect to their SharePoint List.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p162">修复了在法语或德语版的 Excel 中使用 INDIRECT 函数中的 R1C1 样式引用导致 \#REF! 错误，而非生成引用值和预期值的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p162">Fix an issue where using the R1C1-style reference in the INDIRECT function with a French or German version of Excel results in a \#REF! error instead of the referenced and expected value.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-873">修复了在“自定义列表”对话框中创建自定义排序列表时，ENTER 键不能分隔列表条目的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-873">Fix an issue where the ENTER key doesn't work to separate list entries when creating a custom sort list in the Customs Lists dialog box.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p163">修复了复制或移动信息导致出现错误消息的问题（如“无法打开剪贴板”或“无法释放剪贴板上的空间。其他程序可能正在使用它”）。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p163">Fix an issue where copying or moving information causes an error message to appear, such as "Cannot open the Clipboard" or "We couldn't free up space on the Clipboard. -   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-879">解决以下问题：通过使用 Application.OnUndo 保存包含编程撤消级别的工作簿时，工作簿的上次更改被撤消的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-879">Fix an issue where when you save a workbook that includes a programmatic undo level by using Application.OnUndo, the last change to the workbook is undone.</span></span>

### <a name="outlook-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-890">Outlook：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-890">Outlook: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-891">\*\* \@ 提及：\*\* 确保收件人通过将 "@" 符号（后跟人名）添加到 "电子邮件" 或 "日历" 项目的正文中，来知道他们正在要求输入或执行操作。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-891">**\@mentions:** Make sure that recipients know they're being asked for input or action by including the @ symbol followed by the person's name to the body of an email or calendar item.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-892">同时，这也会将他们自动添加到“收件人”行。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-892">This will also automatically add them to the To line.</span></span> [<span data-ttu-id="d47b1-893">更多信息</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-893">More information</span></span>](https://support.office.com/article/90701709-5dc1-41c7-aa48-b01d4a46e8c7)
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p165">**旅游预订和行程的摘要卡：** 使用收件箱和日历中自动创建的摘要卡验证并跟踪旅游预订以及发送行程。 [更多信息](https://blogs.office.com/2016/06/28/stay-on-top-of-your-travel-and-deliveries-with-outlook/)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p165">**Summary cards for travel reservations and packages:** Verify and track travel reservations, as well as package deliveries, using summary cards automatically created in the Inbox and Calendar. -   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-896">**附加照片的微型预览**：将某个照片附加到电子邮件中时，Outlook 在邮件中显示该照片的微型预览。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-896">**Mini-previews for attached photos**: When a photo is attached to an email, Outlook shows a small preview of the photo in the message.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-897">**恢复已删除的邮件链接：** 在“已删除邮件文件夹”中，“恢复最近从此文件夹删除的邮件”链接将显示在已删除邮件列表的上方，在选中该链接后，将打开“恢复已删除邮件”对话框。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-897">**Recover deleted items link:** In the Deleted Items folder, a "Recover items recently removed from this folder" link appears above the list of deleted items, and brings up the Recover Deleted Items dialog box when the link is selected.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p166">**点击：** 从组织的相关文档中查找和重新使用内容。 [详细信息](https://support.office.com/article/860118fc-1f61-41f6-922f-40084a284658)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p166">**Tap:** Find and reuse content from your organization’s relevant documents. [More information](https://support.office.com/article/860118fc-1f61-41f6-922f-40084a284658)</span></span>

### <a name="outlook-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-904">Outlook：非安全更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-904">Outlook: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-905">修复了以下问题：结合使用应用程序虚拟化 (App-V) 和其他应用程序且已设置 AllowJitvInAppvVirtualizedProcess 注册表项时，尝试在控制面板中创建配置文件会导致 Windows 7 发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-905">Fix an issue where a crash occurs on Windows 7 when trying to create profiles from Control Panel when using Application Virtualization (App-V) with other applications and the AllowJitvInAppvVirtualizedProcess registry key is set.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-906">修复了以下问题：会议所有者无法在“跟踪”选项卡中取消选择用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-906">Fix an issue where a meeting owner can't unselect users in the tracking tab.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-907">修复了以下问题：在用户跨多个文件夹执行“高级查找”时，Outlook 发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-907">Fix an issue where Outlook crashes when doing an Advanced Find across multiple folders.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-908">修复了以下问题：在搜索时键入到抄送文本框的文本不会追加到主搜索框，并且无法进行搜索。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-908">Fix an issue where the text typed into the cc text box in a search doesn't get appended to the main search box and a search doesn't occur.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-909">修复了在包含多个带附件的邮件的对话中，尝试打开其中一个邮件的附件时，如果该附件存储在联机位置，则 Outlook 会崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-909">Fix an issue where, in a conversation with multiple messages that have attachments, Outlook crashes when trying to open an attachment in one of those messages, if that attachment is stored in an online location.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-910">修复了以下问题：当用户使用输入法编辑器 (IME) 键入东亚语言字符时，焦点切换到右上角的一个小对话框，导致用户无法继续编辑电子邮件。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-910">Fix an issue where the focus switches to a small dialog box in the upper right corner when typing East Asian characters using an Input Method Editor (IME) and then the user can't continue editing the email message.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-911">修复了以下问题：对带有附件的电子邮件进行数字签名或加密导致附件内容丢失。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-911">Fix an issue where digitally signing or encrypting an email message with an attachment causes the contents of the attachment to be lost.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-912">修复了将自定义母本文档用作默认主题时，多余的换行符被添加到新的电子邮件且字体被设置为 Calibri 的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-912">Fix an issue where, when using customized stationery as the default theme, extra line breaks are added to new email messages and the font is set to Calibri.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-913">修复了如果将 Windows 显示设置为 125%，Outlook 在打开时会冻结的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-913">Fix an issue where Outlook freezes when opening if the Windows display is set to 125%.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-914">修复了粘贴为 OLE 链接的 Excel 单元格从草稿电子邮件消失的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-914">Fix an issue where Excel cells pasted as on OLE link disappear from draft email messages.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-915">修复了用户无法在邮件中预览图像附件的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-915">Fix an issue where users can't preview image attachments in messages.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-916">修复了在 Outlook 2013 或 Outlook 2010 中接收会议邀请时，从 Outlook 2016 发送的会议邀请中图像丢失的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-916">Fix an issue where images in meeting invites sent from Outlook 2016 are missing when received in Outlook 2013 or Outlook 2010.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-917">修复了设计自定义窗体，将字段拖至窗体时导致 Outlook 崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-917">Fix an issue where, when designing a custom form, dragging fields on to the form causes Outlook to crash.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-918">修复了在打开 Outlook 时“文件夹”窗格消失的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-918">Fix an issue where the Folder pane disappears when Outlook is opened.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-919">修复在常用文本字段中使用“高级查找”搜索邮件导致“Outlook 无法执行搜索”错误消息的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-919">Fix an issue where searching messages by using Advanced Find in frequently-used text fields results in an "Outlook cannot perform your search" error message.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-920">修复了在 Microsoft UI 自动化侦听器（例如讲述人）运行时查看会议请求导致 Outlook 崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-920">Fix an issue where viewing a meeting request when a Microsoft UI Automation listener, such as Narrator, is running causes Outlook to crash.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-921">修复在创建某个联系人的新邮件时，即使该联系人的电子邮件地址只有一个，“收件人:”字段仍填充收件人姓名三次的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-921">Fix an issue where, when creating a new message to a contact, the To: field is populated with the recipient's name three times, even though there is only one email address for the contact.</span></span>

### <a name="skype-for-business-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-943">Skype for Business：非安全更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-943">Skype for Business: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-944">修复了以下问题：在 Window 10 版本 1607（亦称为“周年更新”）上，用于共享辅助监视器的选项没有与特定的监视器配置一起显示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-944">Fix an issue where the option to share a secondary monitor doesn't appear with certain monitor configurations on Window 10 Version 1607 (also known as the Anniversary Update).</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-945">修复了以下问题：如果共享者使用第三方 RDP 实现，Skype for Business 在放大共享内容时发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-945">Fix an issue where Skype for Business crashes when zooming into shared content when the sharer is using a 3rd party implementation of RDP.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-p169">修复了以下问题：当 Skype for Business 通过端口 443 连接到 SIP 服务器且存在代理服务器时，如果代理不允许此类连接，登录过程会明显延迟。通过在 HKEY\_CURRENT\_USER\\Software\\Microsoft\\UCCPlatform\\Lync 下添加 EnableDetectProxyForAllConnections DWORD 注册表项，并将值设置为 1，可以启用修复程序。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-p169">Fix an issue where, when Skype for Business connects to a SIP server over port 443 and a proxy server is present, there is a significant delay in the sign-in process if the proxy doesn't allow such connections. The fix is enabled by adding the EnableDetectProxyForAllConnections DWORD registry entry under HKEY\_CURRENT\_USER\\Software\\Microsoft\\UCCPlatform\\Lync, and setting the value to 1.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-948">修复了以下问题：当运行 Windows 7 的用户先共享主监视器，然后切换共享另一台监视器时，出现黑屏。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-948">Fix an issue where viewers see a black screen when a user is running Windows 7 and shares the main monitor first, and then switches to share a second monitor.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-949">修复了以下问题：用户在迁移到 Exchange Online 后，无法通过连接 Exchange 来获取对话历史记录、联系人或语音邮件信息。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-949">Fix an issue where the user can't connect to Exchange to get conversation history, contact, or voicemail information after the user has been migrated to Exchange Online.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-950">修复了以下问题：在对话窗口中，尝试将信息粘贴到拨号盘或白板的文本注释中会错误地将信息粘贴到聊天输入文本框中。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-950">Fix an issue with the conversation window where trying to paste information into the dial pad or into text annotations in the whiteboard incorrectly pastes the information into the chat input text box.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-951">修复了以下问题：在用户使用可更改分辨率的显示器（尤其是高分辨率显示器）时，Skype for Business 不会根据显示器的分辨率变化来更新缩放比例。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-951">Fix an issue where Skype for Business doesn't update scaling with monitor changes when using monitors with different resolutions, especially high resolution monitors.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-952">修复了在使用键盘查看 IM 对话中的参与者列表时，键盘焦点错误地移到聊天历史记录，而非显示参与者列表的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-952">Fix an issue where, when using the keyboard to view the list of participants in an IM conversion, the keyboard focus incorrectly moves to chat history instead of showing the list of participants.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-953">修复了使用高对比度 Windows 主题时，参与者操作屏幕上的工具提示消失的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-953">Fix an issue where the tooltips on the Participant Actions screen disappear when using a high contrast Windows theme.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-954">修复了电话号码的位置未在会议邀请中显示的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-954">Fix an issue where the location of phone numbers isn't shown in meeting invites.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-955">修复了在具有高 DPI 的远程控制方案中的鼠标指针的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-955">Fix an issue with the mouse pointer in remote control scenarios with high DPI.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-956">修复了其他参与者切换显示的共享桌面时，参与者无法看到共享桌面的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-956">Fix an issue where a participant can't see the shared desktop when other participants switch which shared desktop is being displayed.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-957">修复了登录失败并出现证书问题的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-957">Fix an issue where sign in fails with a certificate issue.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-958">修复了从库视图切换到内容视图并切换回库视图时，白板视图不在屏幕顶部加载的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-958">Fix an issue where the Whiteboard View doesn't load at the top of screen when switching from Gallery View to Content View and back to Gallery View.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-959">修复了在 Exchange 进行身份验证期间登录失败的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-959">Fix an issue with sign in failures during Exchange authentication.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-960">修复了当共享资源文件使用 RDP 的第三方实现且共享资源文件的分辨率低于查看器的分辨率时，如果查看器最大化 Skype 窗口，Skype for Business 崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-960">Fix an issue where, when the sharer is using a 3rd party implementation of RDP and the sharer's resolution is lower than the viewer's resolution, Skype for Business crashes if the view maximizes the Skype window.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-961">修复了“内容”按钮在“会议室前端”显示上不工作的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-961">Fix an issue where the Content button doesn't work on the Front of Room display.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-962">修复了在将 Internet Explorer 中的内部代理 pac 文件 URL 配置为自动配置脚本的计算机上重新加入会议失败的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-962">Fix an issuer where rejoining a meeting fails on computers configured for internal proxy pac file URLs in Internet Explorer as an automatic configuration script.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-963">修复了使用键盘快捷方式设置静音或关闭视频时，屏幕阅读器（如讲述人）没有宣布所做的更改的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-963">Fix an issue where, when using keyboard shortcuts to mute or turn off a video, screen readers, such as Narrator, don't announce the changes.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-964">修复了编辑位置对话框没有屏幕阅读器（如讲述人）可以使用的标签的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-964">Fix an issue where the Edit Location dialog box didn't have labels that screen readers, such as Narrator, could use.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-965">修复了屏幕阅读器（如讲述人）未正确处理出现在功能区下方的警报通知的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-965">Fix an issue where screen readers, such as Narrator, don't correctly handle the alert notifications that appear just under the ribbon.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-966">修复了在演示者使用一个或多个超高清显示屏时，基于对等视频的屏幕共享会话导致更高的 CPU 使用率并使应用和操作系统对演示者的计算机的响应不及时的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-966">Fix an issue where a peer-to-peer video-based screen-sharing session causes increased CPU usage and makes apps and the operating system less responsive on the presenter's computer if the presenter is using one or more ultra-high-definition displays.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-967">修复了将 Skype for Business 窗口调整到最小高度导致语音邮件列表不可见的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-967">Fix an issue where resizing the Skype for Business window to the minimum height causes the voice mail list to not be visible.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-968">修复了打开或创建 Skype 会议后单击“会议选项”按钮导致 Outlook 崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-968">Fix an issue where clicking on Meeting Options button after opening or creating a Skype meeting causes Outlook to crash.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-970">修复了在用户更改了 Office 中的默认语言时，主窗口标题的语言未更改的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-970">Fix an issue where the language of the main window title doesn't change if the user changes the default language in Office.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-971">修复了“关系”选项卡向外部联系人显示多次而非仅显示一次的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-971">Fix an issue where the Relationship tab shows an external contact multiple times instead of just once.</span></span>

-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-977">修复了屏幕阅读器不宣布屏幕共享已启动且用户可以看到屏幕的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-977">Fix an issue where a screen reader doesn't announce that screen sharing has started and that people can see the screen.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-978">修复了当用户使用与主持会议的组织无关联的帐户加入会议时，用户看到一个空白对话窗口的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-978">Fix an issue where the user sees a blank conversation window when the user joins a meeting using an account that's not federated with the organization hosting the meeting.</span></span>

### <a name="visio-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-979">Visio：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-979">Visio: Feature updates</span></span>

### <a name="word-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1000">Word：非安全更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1000">Word: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1001">修复了以下问题：如果另存为的目标文件夹包含大量文件（如超过 30,000 个文件），Word 发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1001">Fix an issue where Word crashes when doing a Save As to a folder that contains a large number of files, such as over 30,000 files.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1002">修复了以下问题：使用 InsertXML 方法时，显示的是断开的图片链接占位符，而不是实际图像。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1002">Fix an issue where, when using the InsertXML method, a placeholder for a broken picture link is shown instead of the actual image.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1003">修复了以下问题：如果在另存为操作期间用户在关闭文件后选择了将文件从 Office 文档缓存中删除，Word 发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1003">Fix an issue where Word crashes when doing a Save As and the user has selected the option to delete files from the Office Document Cache when they are closed.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1004">修复了以下问题：如果另存为的目标文件夹包含大量文件（如超过 30,000 个文件），Word 发生故障。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1004">Fix an issue where Word crashes when doing a Save As to a folder that contains a large number of files, such as over 30,000 files.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1005">修复了以下问题：使用 UK 键盘时，按 CTRL+ALT+4 快捷键无法键入欧元符号。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1005">Fix an issue where the CTRL+ALT+4 shortcut doesn't type the Euro sign when using a UK keyboard.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1006">修复了以下问题：当用户使用输入法编辑器 (IME) 键入东亚语言字符时，焦点切换到右上角的一个小对话框，导致用户无法继续编辑文档。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1006">Fix an issue where the focus switches to a small dialog box in the upper right corner when typing East Asian characters using an Input Method Editor (IME) and then the user can't continue editing the document.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1007">修复了以下问题：使用日语输入法编辑器 (IME) 输入双字节字符集 (DBCS) 符号字符时，字体更改为 Segoe UI 表情符号。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1007">Fix an issue where the font is changed to Segoe UI Emoji when inputting double-byte character set (DBCS) symbol characters when using the Japanese input method editor (IME).</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1008">修复了在用户尝试将博客文章发布到 SharePoint 时，系统错误地提示用户提供博客主凭据的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1008">Fix an issue where the user is incorrectly prompted to provide Blogger credentials when trying to publish a blog post to SharePoint.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1009">修复了用户更改默认编辑或校对语言时，该更改未在下次 Word 打开时继承的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1009">Fix an issue that when the user changes the default editing or proofing language, that change doesn't carry over to the next time Word is opened.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1010">修复在需要基于表单的身份验证的服务器上打开文档导致 Word 崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1010">Fix an issue where opening a document on a server that requires forms-based authentication causes Word to crash.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite-feature-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1011">Office 套件：功能更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1011">Office suite: Feature updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1012">**共享计算机激活的许可令牌续订：** Office 尝试在令牌 50% 到期时立即定期为共享计算机激活续订许可令牌，以帮助并非总是拥有 Internet 访问权限的用户。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1012">**Licensing token renewal for shared computer activation:** Office attempts to renew the licensing token for shared computer activation on a regular basis once the token is 50% expired, to help users who don't always have Internet access.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1013">**共享计算机激活的缩减功能模式：** 使用共享计算机激活时，如果用户关闭了登录窗口或用户的许可令牌到期，用户仍可以使用 Office 应用，但应用将处于缩减功能模式。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1013">**Reduced functionality mode for shared computer activation:** When using shared computer activation, if the user closes the sign-in window or the user's licensing token expires, the user can still use the Office app, but the app will be in reduced functionality mode.</span></span>

### <a name="office-suite-non-security-updates"></a><span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1019">Office 套件：非安全更新</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1019">Office suite: Non-security updates</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1020">修复了以下问题：使用 VBA 窗体可能会导致框架的 z 顺序无法正常运行或显示。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1020">Fix an issue with VBA forms that can cause the z-order of frames to stop functioning or display incorrectly.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1021">修复了以下问题：配置管理器触发的更新将注册表中的 UpdateChannel 设置更改为不是有效更新通道的内容。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1021">Fix an issue where an update trigged by Configuration Manager changes the UpdateChannel setting in the registry to something that's not a valid update channel.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1022">修复了以下问题：使用 OneDrive 同步客户端将文件从 OneDrive for Business 网站同步到本地计算机时，保存通过 URL 打开的同步返回文件导致 Word、Excel 或 PowerPoint 挂起。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1022">Fix an issue where, when files are synced from a OneDrive for Business site to a local computer using the OneDrive sync client, saving a synced back file that was opened from a URL causes Word, Excel, or PowerPoint to hang.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1023">修复了以下问题：VBA 表单控件可导致透明标签控件显示为不透明；现有表单不再按预期方式显示或运行；尝试打开包含表单控件的启用宏的文件时，Office 应用程序停止响应。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1023">Fix an issue with VBA form controls that can cause transparent label controls to appear opaque, can cause existing forms to no longer appear or work as expected, and can cause the Office application to stop responding when attempting to open a macro-enabled file that contains form controls.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1024">修复了使用托管元数据属性时，“显示详细信息”按钮显示在“文件”\>“信息”下的“属性”部分，而不是设置的元数据值的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1024">Fix an issue where, when using managed metadata properties, a "Show Details" button appears in the Properties section under File \> Info instead of the metadata values that are set.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1025">修复了在使用操作说明搜索时，选择“获取帮助”后“帮助”窗格显示为单独的对话框而不显示在应用程序中的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1025">Fix an issue where the Help pane appears as a separate dialog box, instead of within the application, when selecting Get Help when using Tell Me.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1026">修复了 OfficeC2RClient.exe 不将“频道”识别为可选设置的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1026">Fix an issue where OfficeC2RClient.exe doesn't recognize "channel" as an optional setting.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1027">修复了新版本和内部版本格式不会显示在“文件”\>“帐户”下的 Office Update 中的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1027">Fix an issue where the new version and build format doesn't show in the Office Updates section under File \> Account.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1028">修复了切换到不同的更新频道可能会导致下次运行更新过程时会安装较早的内部版本的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1028">Fix an issue where switching to a different update channel may result in an earlier build being installed the next time the update process is run.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1029">修复了以下问题：使用 GDI 打印机驱动程序 V3 版本的打印机无法打印。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1029">Fix an issue with printing to printers that use a V3 version of the GDI printer driver.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1030">修复了以下问题：执行联机修复时看不到安装用户界面 (UI)。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1030">Fix an issue where the installation user interface (UI) doesn't appear when performing an Online Repair.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1031">修复了即使对联机模板的访问权限已被组策略设置或注册表设置禁用，“联机模板搜索”框仍然启用的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1031">Fix an issue where the "Search for online templates" box is still enabled even after access to online templates has been disabled by a Group Policy setting or a registry setting.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1032">修复了了打开 Office 应用时，用户收到错误消息“Microsoft 无法找到应用程序的许可证，且修复尝试已失败或取消”，然后 Office 应用关闭的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1032">Fix an issue where, when opening an Office app, the user receives an error message that Microsoft can't find the license for the application and that a repair attempt was unsuccessful or cancelled, and then the Office app closes.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1033">修复了二进制增量压缩导致之前内部版本的更新程序下载大小大于其应有大小的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1033">Fix an issue with binary delta compression causing the size of the downloads for the updates for the previous build to be larger than they should be.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1034">修复了 Office Update 任务运行过于频繁，导致 CPU 使用率的增长以及桌面图标短暂闪烁或刷新的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1034">Fix an issue where the Office Update task runs too frequently, causing increased CPU usage and desktop icons to briefly flash or refresh.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1035">修复了多个用户同时在一台具有特定权限配置的计算机上运行 Office 导致 Office 应用崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1035">Fix an issue where multiple users running Office at the same time on a single computer with a specific permissions configuration causes Office apps to crash.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1036">修复使用 Office 外接程序命令导致 Excel、Word 或 PowerPoint 随机崩溃的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1036">Fix an issue where using Office add-in commands causes Excel, Word, or PowerPoint to randomly crash.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1037">修复了更新 Office 会覆盖 ODBC 注册表项并要求安装或修复 Microsoft Access 数据库引擎可再发行的问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1037">Fix an issue where updating Office overwrites ODBC registry entries and requires the Microsoft Access Database Engine Redistributable to be reinstalled or repaired.</span></span>
-   <span data-ttu-id="d47b1-1038">修复了从 URL（例如从 SharePoint 和以 / 字符结尾的 URL）打开 Office 文档时的 PowerPoint、Word 或 Excel 崩溃问题。</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d47b1-1038">Fix an issue where PowerPoint, Word, or Excel crashes when an Office document is opened from a URL, such as from SharePoint, and the URL ends with the / character.</span></span>
